***подмывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подмывать.html>подмыва́ть</a> (18582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмыть.html>подмы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podmýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмывать.html>подмыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podmyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмыть.html>подмы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash (an individual body part, e.g. the armpit)</li>
<li>to wash hastily, to in separate places</li>
<li>to wash away, to erode, to undermine <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to desire strongly, to be tempted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подмывать.html>подмыва́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá tak i <b>podmyválo</b> kričátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was so <b>tempted</b> to scream</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подмыва́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podmyvátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подмы́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podmýtʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подмы́вка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podmývka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***подмыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подмыть.html>подмыть</a> (27273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мыть.html>мыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмыть.html>подмы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podmýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмывать.html>подмыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash (an individual body part, e.g. the armpit)</li>
<li>to wash hastily, to in separate places</li>
<li>to wash away, to erode, to undermine <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подмышка.html>подмы́шка</a> (12147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">under</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышка.html>мы́шка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mýška</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">"mouse", meaning "muscle" (see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышца.html>мы́шца</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mýšca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for more)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмышка.html>подмы́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podmýška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмышка.html>подмы́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмышка.html>подмы́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмышка.html>подмы́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> armpit, underarm
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нюхать.html>ню́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волосатый.html>волоса́тые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подмышка.html>подмы́шки</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú njúxatʹ jevó volosátyje <b>podmýški</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I want to sniff his hairy <b>armpits</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прятать.html>пря́чу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышка.html>мы́шкой</a></strong>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja prjaču knigu pod myškoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I hide a book in my <b>armpits</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подниматься.html>поднима́ться</a> (1151)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднимать.html>поднима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подниматься.html>поднима́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnimátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подняться.html>подня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rise, to go up, to get up</li>
<li>to ascend, to climb</li>
<li>to arise, to break out, to develop, to set out, to get agitated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve, to recover</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднимать.html>поднима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***подноготная.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подноготная.html>подного́тная</a> (27375)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноготь.html>но́готь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nógotʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From "<a href = vnd.unilang:подноготная.html>подного́тная</a> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">právda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>" - "the truth from under the fingernails", extracted by torture in the ancient times.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подноготная.html>подного́тная</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnogótnaja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">feminine nominative singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подноготный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnogotnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подноготная.html>подного́тная</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnogótnaja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подноготная.html>подного́тной</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>lowdown, ins and outs
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подноготная.html>подного́тную</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Uznátʹ vsju <b>podnogótnuju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">To find out all the whole truth (e.g. about a person).</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подножка.html>подно́жка</a> (9369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подножка.html>подно́жка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnóžka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подножка.html>подно́жки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подножка.html>подно́жки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подножка.html>подно́жек</a></b>)

<li>trip, back heel

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подносить.html>подноси́ть</a> (8813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подносить.html>подноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднести.html>поднести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring, to carry (to)</li>
<li>to offer, to present</li></ol>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поднятие.html>подня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>фла́га</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podnjátije</b> flága</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">hoisting a flag; making the colours</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднимать.html>поднима́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подняться.html>подня́ться</a> (476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подняться.html>подня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подниматься.html>поднима́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rise, to go up, to get up</li>
<li>to ascend, to climb</li>
<li>to arise, to break out, to develop, to set out, to get agitated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve, to recover</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подобать.html>подоба́ть</a> (12384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобать.html>подоба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podobátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to become, to befit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подобать.html>подоба́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поступать.html>поступа́ть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>podobájet</b> tak postupátʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it doesn't become one to behave like that; such behaviour/conduct is unbecoming</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
